[2025-12-26T01:45:05Z] Naman Agarwal: Hi folks, I am thinking of the following quiz format for a quiz that I am writing. The quiz has equal number of questions from two categories (Bollywood and cricket). I am thinking of 24 questions total. The quiz has 6 participants, 3 participants are cricket experts and 3 participants are Bollywood experts. Every one is competing against each other but each person is uniquely matched to a person with the opposite expertise. ↵ The quiz is now a standard Infy bounce still but with two additional rules ↵ if you get a question with your expertise you can score whatever you score but you also get half the negatives of what you can't score (in case of partial marks) ↵ If you get a question for the other category, you have the option of (before attempting any part) to transfer it to your 'partner' and whatever points they score gets divided half between you and them. This transfer is an optional privilege, you can choose to attempt or pass the question. ↵ Do you guys see a flaw with the format? ‎<This message was edited>
